       page = OsVmPhysPagesAlloc(seg, nPages);// 分配连续内存\r\n        if (page != NULL) {\r\n            /* the first page of continuous physical addresses holds refCounts */\r\n            LOS_AtomicSet(\u0026page-\u003ErefCounts, 0);\r\n            page-\u003EnPages = nPages;// 记载页数\r\n```\r\n释放时按此记录将内存退还空闲链表。\r\n\r\n问题：OsVmPhysPagesAlloc实际分配的可能不是nPages页，而是其向上取整2的整数幂，如nPages=5则实际分配8页(2^3)。这样就可能出现内存泄漏：有8-5=3页内存不会被退还空闲块链表，从而不再能被使用。\r\n\r\n修复这个问题有两种策略：一是多分配，即记录修正为实际分配的2的整数幂；二是按需分配，即修正分配函数OsVmPhysPagesAlloc不产生多余的页。这里采用后一种。","assignees_number":1,"testers_number":1,"assignees":[{"id":7920580,"login":"kkup180","name":"likailong","avatar_url":"https://gitee.com/assets/no_portrait.png","url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180","html_url":"https://gitee.com/kkup180","followers_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/followers","following_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/following_url{/other_user}","gists_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/gists{/gist_id}","starred_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/starred{/owner}{/repo}","subscriptions_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/subscriptions","organizations_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/orgs","repos_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/repos","events_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/events{/privacy}","received_events_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/received_events","type":"User"},{"id":8063914,"login":"wangmihu2008","name":"wangmihu","avatar_url":"https://gitee.com/assets/no_portrait.png","url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008","html_url":"https://gitee.com/wangmihu2008","followers_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/followers","following_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/following_url{/other_user}","gists_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/gists{/gist_id}","starred_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/starred{/owner}{/repo}","subscriptions_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/subscriptions","organizations_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/orgs","repos_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/repos","events_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/events{/privacy}","received_events_url":"https        page = OsVmPhysPagesAlloc(seg, nPages);// 分配连续内存\r\n        if (page != NULL) {\r\n            /* the first page of continuous physical addresses holds refCounts */\r\n            LOS_AtomicSet(\u0026page-\u003ErefCounts, 0);\r\n            page-\u003EnPages = nPages;// 记载页数\r\n```\r\n释放时按此记录将内存退还空闲链表。\r\n\r\n问题：OsVmPhysPagesAlloc实际分配的可能不是nPages页，而是其向上取整2的整数幂，如nPages=5则实际分配8页(2^3)。这样就可能出现内存泄漏：有8-5=3页内存不会被退还空闲块链表，从而不再能被使用。\r\n\r\n修复这个问题有两种策略：一是多分配，即记录修正为实际分配的2的整数幂；二是按需分配，即修正分配函数OsVmPhysPagesAlloc不产生多余的页。这里采用后一种。\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n","assignees_number":1,"testers_number":1,"assignees":[{"id":7920580,"login":"kkup180","name":"likailong","avatar_url":"https://gitee.com/assets/no_portrait.png","url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180","html_url":"https://gitee.com/kkup180","followers_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/followers","following_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/following_url{/other_user}","gists_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/gists{/gist_id}","starred_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/starred{/owner}{/repo}","subscriptions_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/subscriptions","organizations_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/orgs","repos_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/repos","events_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/events{/privacy}","received_events_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/received_events","type":"User"},{"id":8063914,"login":"wangmihu2008","name":"wangmihu","avatar_url":"https://gitee.com/assets/no_portrait.png","url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008","html_url":"https://gitee.com/wangmihu2008","followers_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/followers","following_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/following_url{/other_user}","gists_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/gists{/gist_id}","starred_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/starred{/owner}{/repo}","subscriptions_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/subscriptions","organizations_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/orgs","repos_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/repos","events_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/events{/privacy}","received_ev 1. 优化OsVmRegionSplit结点操作。https://gitee.com/openharmony/kernel_liteos_a/blob/master/kernel/base/vm/los_vm_map.c#L661\r\n\r\n现在的操作顺序是先删除oldRegion，然后调整其大小，如果大小不为0再加回来。红黑树结点增删较费时，删后再增是不合适的。因此调整操作顺序为先调整大小，如果为0再删除。\r\n\r\n##### 2. 修改OsVmRegionAdjust起始地址不在某region时的行为。https://gitee.com/openharmony/kernel_liteos_a/blob/master/kernel/base/vm/los_vm_map.c#L685\r\n\r\n现在的代码逻辑是，如果传入的newRegionStart不在某个region就报错返回，这限制了函数的用途，如调用链：OsVmRegionAdjust \u003C- OsRegionsRemove \u003C- OsUnMMap \u003C- LOS_UnMMap \u003C- OsAllocSpecificRange，最后一个函数(https://gitee.com/openharmony/kernel_liteos_a/blob/master/kernel/base/vm/los_vm_map.c#L406)在起始地址或结束地址或一段地址属于某region时，都将使用这个调用链，显然两种情形将失败。\r\n\r\n分析该函数的使用场景，逻辑应调整为：起始地址不在某region时，就继续处理结束地址。代码修改看起来挺多，实际就将一个语句改换了位置。\r\n\r\n##### ，以允许没有硬件的开发。这组PR为虚拟Cortex-A7单板添加了BSP，由QEMU和该单板的专用目标进行仿真，因此输出映像可以在仿真平台上运行。目前只允许调试生成，所以OHOS引导到shell。目前还没有文件系统驱动程序，所以唯一可用的功能是shell中嵌入的命令。\r\n\r\nIt would be nice to boot OpenHarmony in QEMU to allow        page = OsVmPhysPagesAlloc(seg, nPages);// 分配连续内存\r\n        if (page != NULL) {\r\n            /* the first page of continuous physical addresses holds refCounts */\r\n            LOS_AtomicSet(\u0026page-\u003ErefCounts, 0);\r\n            page-\u003EnPages = nPages;// 记载页数\r\n```\r\n释放时按此记录将内存退还空闲链表。问题是OsVmPhysPagesAlloc实际分配的可能不是nPages页，而是其向上取整2的整数幂，如nPages=5则实际分配8页(2^3)。这样就出现了内存泄漏问题：有8-5=3页内存不会被退还空闲块链表，从页不再能被使用。\r\n\r\n修复这个问题有两种策略：一是多分配，即记录修正为实际分配的2的整数幂；二是按需分配，即修正分配函数OsVmPhysPagesAlloc不产生多余的页。这里采用后一种。\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n","assignees_number":1,"testers_number":1,"assignees":[{"id":7920580,"login":"kkup180","name":"likailong","avatar_url":"https://gitee.com/assets/no_portrait.png","url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180","html_url":"https://gitee.com/kkup180","followers_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/followers","following_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/following_url{/other_user}","gists_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/gists{/gist_id}","starred_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/starred{/owner}{/repo}","subscriptions_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/subscriptions","organizations_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/orgs","repos_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/repos","events_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/events{/privacy}","received_events_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/kkup180/received_events","type":"User"},{"id":8063914,"login":"wangmihu2008","name":"wangmihu","avatar_url":"https://gitee.com/assets/no_portrait.png","url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008","html_url":"https://gitee.com/wangmihu2008","followers_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/followers","following_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/following_url{/other_user}","gists_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/gists{/gist_id}","starred_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/starred{/owner}{/repo}","subscriptions_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/subscriptions","organizations_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/orgs","repos_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/repos","events_url":"https://gitee.com/api/v5/users/wangmihu2008/events{/privacy}","received_events_ur
